It has a private location just off Buck Creek Rd surrounded by nature''s beauty. The original home began as a manufactured home, but that isn''t visible from the inside or out due to the add-ons and remodeling done in later years. Inside an awesome custom staircase leads to a 2nd level bedroom, but everything else is located on the main. Enjoy the peace &amp; mountain views from a wraparound deck. There''s an addtl building on the property for workshop &amp; storage. Sold As-Is, &amp; Sellers motivated.
